# Grist API Reference

REST API for manipulating documents, workspaces, and team sites.

- [API Usage](rest-api.md) is an introduction to using the API.
- [API Console](https://docs.getgrist.com/apiconsole) allows you to make API calls from the browser.
</div>

</div></div></div></div><div id="section/Authentication" data-section-id="section/Authentication" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#section/Authentication" aria-label="section/Authentication"></a>Authentication</h1></div></div><div id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" data-section-id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#section/Authentication/ApiKey" aria-label="section/Authentication/ApiKey"></a>ApiKey</h2><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>Access to the Grist API is controlled by an Authorization header, which should contain the word &#39;Bearer&#39;, followed by a space, followed by your API key.</p>
</div><div class="sc-gsWcmt gFFElt"><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>Security Scheme Type: </b><span>HTTP</span></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>HTTP Authorization Scheme: </b><code>bearer</code></div><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>Bearer format: </b><code>Authorization: Bearer XXXXXXXXXXX</code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/orgs" aria-label="tag/orgs"></a>orgs</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Team sites and personal spaces are called &#39;orgs&#39; in the API.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/listOrgs" id="operation/listOrgs" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" aria-label="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs"></a>List the orgs you have access to<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/orgs</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/orgs</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>This enumerates all the team sites or personal areas available.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>An array of organizations</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Response samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn iwcKgn cAqMTE hTttpy" kind="field" title="delta"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">delta</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">object</span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-eJocfa jWaWWE bArHDh"> (<!-- -->DocAccessWrite<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Success</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" data-section-id="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/downloadTableSchema" id="operation/downloadTableSchema" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" aria-label="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema"></a>The schema of a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/download/table-schema</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/download/table-schema</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>The schema follows <a href="https://specs.frictionlessdata.io/table-schema/">frictionlessdata&#39;s table-schema standard</a>.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Name of a table (normalized).</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="header"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">header</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;colId&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;label&quot;</span> </div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Format for headers. Labels tend to be more human-friendly while colIds are more normalized.</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/records" data-section-id="tag/records" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/records" aria-label="tag/records"></a>records</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Tables contain collections of records (also called rows).</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/records/operation/listRecords" data-section-id="tag/records/operation/listRecords" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/listRecords" id="operation/listRecords" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/records/operation/listRecords" aria-label="tag/records/operation/listRecords"></a>Fetch records from a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="hidden"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">hidden</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to include the hidden columns (like &quot;manualSort&quot;)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="noparse"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">noparse</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to prohibit parsing strings according to the column type.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="onmany"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">onmany</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;first&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;none&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">&quot;all&quot;</span> </div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Which records to update if multiple records are found to match <code>require</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>first</code> - the first matching record (default)</li>
<li><code>none</code> - do not update anything</li>
<li><code>all</code> - update all matches</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="noadd"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">noadd</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to prohibit adding records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="noupdate"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">noupdate</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to prohibit updating records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="allow_empty_require"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">allow_empty_require</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Set to true to allow <code>require</code> in the body to be empty, which will match and update all records in the table.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>The records to add or update. Instead of an id, a <code>require</code> object is provided, with the same structure as <code>fields</code>. If no query parameter options are set, then the operation is as follows. First, we check if a record exists matching the values specified for columns in <code>require</code>. If so, we update it by setting the values specified for columns in <code>fields</code>. If not, we create a new record with a combination of the values in <code>require</code> and <code>fields</code>, with <code>fields</code> taking priority if the same column is specified in both. The query parameters allow for variations on this behavior.</p>
</div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn iwcKgn cAqMTE hTttpy" kind="field" title="records"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">records</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa">Array of </span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">objects</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </div></div></div><div id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" data-section-id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/getTableData" id="operation/getTableData" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data/operation/getTableData" aria-label="tag/data/operation/getTableData"></a>Fetch data from a table<!-- --> <span type="warning" class="sc-bqGGPW eSYQnm"> Deprecated </span></h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>records</code> endpoints. We have no immediate plans to remove these endpoints, but consider <code>records</code> a better starting point for new projects.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Cells from the table</p>

data-section-id="tag/data/operation/modifyRows" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/modifyRows" id="operation/modifyRows" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data/operation/modifyRows" aria-label="tag/data/operation/modifyRows"></a>Modify rows of a table<!-- --> <span type="warning" class="sc-bqGGPW eSYQnm"> Deprecated </span></h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="patch" class="sc-fmdNqN cDAiVX http-verb patch">patch</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" QGruV"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>records</code> endpoints. We have no immediate plans to remove these endpoints, but consider <code>records</code> a better starting point for new projects.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>

</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>the IDs of rows to remove</p>
</div><div><div class="sc-bCwfaz jaCkRh"> Array </div><div class="sc-hmbstg gBTJlj"><div><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">integer</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iwajpm kHKMOg"></div></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>Nothing returned</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="react-tabs__tab react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-80" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-81" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">Payload</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-81" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-80"><div><div class="sc-Arkif jojbRz"><span class="sc-cOifOu hlhNtL">Content type</span><div class="sc-bBjRSN kQSIAz">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-jgPyTC dSaTNC"><div class="sc-jNnpgg esZIbL"><div class="sc-giAqHp hMPeqJ"><button><div class="sc-carFqZ UksDl">Copy</div></button></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE jCdxGr sc-dPaNzc gyljjx"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="array collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">101</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">102</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">103</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">]</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs bpZWeL"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments" aria-label="tag/attachments"></a>attachments</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN lksXXu"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV redoc-markdown "><p>Documents may include attached files. Data records can refer to these using a column of type <code>Attachments</code>.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/listAttachments" id="operation/listAttachments" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" aria-label="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments"></a>List metadata of all attachments in a doc<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN ihNycv http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/docs/{docId}/attachments</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf fcvuS"><span class="sc-dsXzNU dPrSxx"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>Query options</p>
</div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="sql"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">sql</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>The SQL query to run. Must be a single SELECT statement, with no trailing semicolon. WITH clauses are permitted. All Grist documents are currently SQLite databases, and the SQL query is interpreted and run by SQLite, with various defensive measures. Statements that would modify the database are not supported.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn iwcKgn cAqMTE hTttpy" kind="field" title="args"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">args</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa">Array of </span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">numbers or strings</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Parameters for the query.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="timeout"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">timeout</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>Timeout after which operations on the document will be interrupted. Specified in milliseconds. Defaults to 1000 (1 second). This default is controlled by an optional environment variable read by the Grist app, GRIST_SQL_TIMEOUT_MSEC. The default cannot be exceeded, only reduced.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>The result set for the query.</p>

</div></div></div><div id="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" data-section-id="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN bwFyQs"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM eftmgB"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" aria-label="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete"></a>Delete a user from Grist<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="delete" class="sc-fmdNqN bJzUtf http-verb delete">delete</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT fCEUju">/users/{userId}</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dfUAUz"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/users/{userId}</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"><p>This action also deletes the user&#39;s personal organisation and all the workspaces and documents it contains.
Currently, only the users themselves are allowed to delete their own accounts.</p>
<p>⚠️ <strong>This action cannot be undone, please be cautious when using this endpoint</strong> ⚠️</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr QGruV"></div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="name"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">name</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>The user&#39;s name to delete (for confirmation, to avoid deleting the wrong account).</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC eDjFAZ"><p>The account has been deleted successfully</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy bummOK gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT iwcKgn cAqMTE" kind="field" title="count"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bcnRwz"></span><span class="property-name">count</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK ctPuOP"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">integer</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE fElSEN">count=10</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr lhENGb"><p>The number of users to retrieve.</p>
